function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 611') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.611!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// File added: userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir') && (sha1_file('userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir');
	$tmp = pathinfo('userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir');
} else if (sha1_file('userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of userdata/attachments/oidplus_upload.dir');
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '66e8325cbc063eacfe314974b94f04d73a7ced7d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '66e8325cbc063eacfe314974b94f04d73a7ced7d') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '3dcf6c9de9ed4e16ab3e044d4a66fd6616fe0c97') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '66e8325cbc063eacfe314974b94f04d73a7ced7d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
